_318	Rules/circulars			Lisa Morris-Sobczynska	2008-01-13	Odile Martin	2008-01-30	EN-GB	p	fiche en compte	A CERN slip, allowing members of the personnel (especially those just arriving) to obtain an advance on their next month's salary. Via the slilp, CERN guarantees that a given sum will be paid into the person's account - as a salary payment - on a given date, and the UBS allows him to withdraw money on that basis, even though his account does not currently contain that amount. The associated costs (charged at the UBS unauthorized overdraft rate) are borne by the person concerned. Department FI/F.	Lisa Morris-Sobczynska	2008-01-13	Lisa Morris-Sobczynska	2008-01-13
